continue but make sure that BlackJack and Texas Holdem are also active. I added one thing to Rhum32. It is multiplayer options. You need to understand the logic of online poker games such as Zynga Texas Holdem so that you could apply to my gameplay: Game Play 1. Follow the rules as outlined above. 2. When a player selects Rhum 32 from the Dashboard, there must be Multiplayer or Single Player options. 3. Multiplayer should allow you to invite friends or join a table. 4. For each option you must see table options similar to SipSam and you must have a minimum Bank to enter each table: Table Value Minimum Bank to Enter $100 $3000 $500 $15000 $1000 $25000 $5000 $100000 VIP- $10000 $1000000 Table 5- Table Entry Requirements 5. Once they select a table that they qualify for, they must be able to invite friends similar to SipSam. The Invite Field should load their existing friends and they must be able to instantaneously send an invite that expires in 3 minutes. 6. The player could start the table without their invited friends. Friends can join later once the invite has not expired. 7. If friends do not meet the minimum bank required for that table, they will be notified in your invitation to them to join your game. They will be given options to earn chips through ads. 8. A single player could start a game. 9. Strangers must be able to join games if seats are available similar to online Poker games. The channel for this is in the Multiplayer options from point 3 above. 10. The Dealer will always be a Bot. Players cannot be the dealer. However, players must be given random seats at the table. Remember that each table only has a maximum of 6 players. We must ensure that multiple tables exist for each Table value eg $100, $500 etc. 11. Players are given 10 seconds to place bets including the Tie Bet. Once this 10 seconds end, the first four (4) cards are dealt. Players will be allowed to freeze or unfreeze bets when cards start dealing and during the course of rounds. When you unfreeze your bet, betting options will be available after the round ends. This is, of course, the same betting period of 10 seconds. 12. Players are given another 10 seconds to place their Back Bets if they decide to continue the round. In this case they will be given 2 options: a. Push- this is if they no longer wish to participate in that round b. Bet- the Back Bet is automatically placed from their wallet 13. If a player plays the Front Bet and cannot back up the Back Bet because their wallet is depleted, they are disqualified. They will be able to sit one more round as an observer. If they do not replenish their wallet during this round, they will be terminated from the table. 14. During Game Play, players must be able to: a. Invite friends similar to SipSam b. Chat using chat bubbles similar to SipSam c. Replenish their Wallet from their Bank similar to SipSam d. Send chips to players on the table e. Request chips from players on the table f. Exit the game. Once you leave, the remaining money in your wallet is returned to your bank. 15. The system determines the outcome of each game and controls all the logics including payments.

This session is being continued from a previous conversation that ran out of context. The summary below covers the earlier portion of the conversation. Summary: 1. Primary Request and Intent: - User wants to add **Rhum32** card game to the vurglife-platform collection, following the same architecture as the existing SipSam game - Rhum32 is a Caribbean casino card game: 1 deck, up to 6 players vs a house Dealer bot, goal is hand value less than dealer's, dealer busts over 32 - User provided a detailed development document (Rhum32 Development.docx) with complete rules, payment tables, specials (A-5, 0, 1-5, 4-7, 8-11, 12-17, 18-31, 47-50 specials), and table configurations - User later added **multiplayer requirements** (15-point spec): mode select (multiplayer/single player), browse/join open tables like Zynga poker, invite friends with 3-minute expiry, strangers can join, max 6 players per table, multiple table instances per tier, dealer always bot, freeze bets, chat, chip transfer, replenish wallet, exit game - User explicitly stated **BlackJack and Texas Hold'em already exist** and do NOT need to be built — they just need to be made **active** on the dashboard (not "coming soon") 2. Key Technical Concepts: - **Architecture**: Express HTTP server (matchmake API) + separate WebSocket server (game logic), proxied through VurgLife platform on port 3000 - **SipSam pattern**: Port 2999 Express + Port 3001 WebSocket; Rhum32: Port 2998 Express + Port 3002 WebSocket - **Multi-table RoomManager**: Creates/destroys room instances per table tier, supports browse/join/create/quick-join - **Game phases**: waiting → betting (10s) → dealing4 → decision (10s) → dealing5 → revealing → roundEnd - **Card zero rules**: 3-of-a-kind, 4-of-a-kind, and straight flush of 3+ cards in same suit all count as 0 - **Payment tiers**: Front bet always 1:1; Back bet multipliers range from 1:1 (normal) to 100:1 (A-5 Special) - **Table tiers**: $100, $500, $1000, $5000, VIP $10000 with corresponding minimum banks - **Friends system**: FriendDB already exists in database.js with sendRequest/accept/getFriends/areFriends methods - **Invite system**: In-memory Map with 3-minute TTL, notifications via NotifDB - **Existing games in main repo**: BlackJack (port 3002 WS), Texas Hold'em (port 3004 WS) — fully built with servers and clients 3. Files and Code Sections: **CREATED - rhum32-server/logic.js** - Core game logic engine: card values (A=1, 2-9 face, T/J/Q/K=10), zero-rule detection, hand value calculation, special detection (A-5, 0, face card 47-50), payment tier resolution, player vs dealer resolution - Key exports: createDeck, shuffleDeck, cardValue, findZeroCards, calculateHandValue, isA5Special, isStraightFlush5, checkFaceCardSpecial, getPaymentTier, resolvePlayerVsDealer, dealCards **CREATED - rhum32-server/Rhum32Room.js** - Full game room class with phases, timers, player management - Static TABLE_CONFIG with 5 tiers (100, 500, 1000, 5000, 10000) - Message dispatch: startGame, placeBet, placeTieBet, playerDecision, freezeBet, requestState, sendChips, requestChips, chat - Game flow: startRound → dealFourCards → autoDecide → dealFifthCard → resolveRound → endGame - Public state filtering: hides other players' cards and dealer hidden cards **CREATED - rhum32-server/RoomManager.js** - The fix: changed justify-content from center to flex-start with padding. When justify-content: center is used with flex-column and the content is taller than the viewport, it pushes the top of the card above the screen edge — making everything invisible since overflow was hidden. Using flex-start with top padding prevents that.

Redirecting to VurgLife dashboard..." and won't load the lobby 2. Key Technical Concepts: - **Architecture**: VurgLife platform (port 3000) auto-starts all game servers via child_process spawn - **Port assignments**: SipSam WS=3001, BlackJack WS=3002, Rhum32 WS=3003, Hold'em WS=3004, SipSam API=2999, Rhum32 API=2998 - **Session passing**: Dashboard stores user/table data in sessionStorage, game clients read it on DOMContentLoaded and redirect to / if missing - **Direct entry pattern** (BlackJack/Hold'em/Rhum32): enterXTable() directly sets sessionStorage and does window.location.href — no ad modal - **SipSam-style invite**: Type-ahead input field that shows friends dropdown on focus, searches all players after 350ms delay - **sql.js database**: Uses run, get, all helper functions (not native sqlite3) 3. Files and Code Sections: - **G:\SipSam\PokerProject\rhum32-client\game.js** (MOST CRITICAL - current issue) - Contains DOMContentLoaded auto-login handler that reads rhum32_user from sessionStorage - If not found, calls window.location.replace('/') which may be failing/stuck - Key auto-login code: ```javascript window.addEventListener('DOMContentLoaded', function() { try { const userJson = sessionStorage.getItem('rhum32_user'); const tableJson = sessionStorage.getItem('rhum32_table'); if (!userJson) { window.location.replace('/'); return; } const user = JSON.parse(userJson); if (!user || !user.username) { window.location.replace('/'); return; } // ... sets globals, populates lobby banner ... showScreen('screen-lobby'); } catch(e) { window.location.replace('/'); } }); ``` - Lobby functions: selectMode(), selectRounds(), updateLobbyInfo(), startGame() - SipSam-style invite: getLobbyFriends(), searchAllPlayers(), onLobbyInviteInput(), renderLobbyDropdown(), onLobbyInviteFocus(), selectLobbyInvitee(), sendLobbyInvite() - Game functions: createAndJoinTable(), startSinglePlayer(), joinRoom() - SERVER_HTTP = "http://localhost:3000", SERVER_WS = "ws://localhost:3003" - **G:\SipSam\PokerProject\rhum32-client\index.html** - screen-login: Shows "Connecting... Verify the following; if not already implemented, I need you to implement: The main Rule for Bots is based on an assumption: 1. The dealer turns up 1 card and the rest is face down. This means 3 cards are face down. The assumption is that the sum of the 3 faced down cards is twenty (20). a. If the dealer shows a face up card of value 10, this means that the assumption is that the total value of their four (4) cards is the sum of the turned down cards (assumed to be 20) + the face up card (10) and this gives an assumed value of 30. b. Once a face up card shows (value of 10), everyone bets. This is because the dealer is assumed to have 30 and most likely will ‘Bust’ (cross 32). c. Therefore, the assumed value of the Dealer’s four (4) cards is always 20 + the value of the face up card. d. If the dealer shows an Ace, it is assumed they have a total of 21 with their first four cards. This is usually a risky play. e. Players bet based on the value of their cards vs the assumed value of the Dealer’s cards. If the Dealer turns up an Ace, we assume that they currently have 21. If we have 24 or higher, this becomes very risky. f. Some players are willing to still bet if they have a value that is 2 scores higher than the Dealer’s assumed value. For example, the Dealer shows an Ace and the player has 23. It is assumed that the Dealer has 21 so the player continues to play with their 23 since it is only 2 scores more than 21. g. Some players never bet if they have more than the Dealer’s assumed value. For example, if the Dealer shows a 5, the assumed value is 25 and the player holding cards valued at 26 or more will not player. Some players still play if they have a value of cards that is 1 score higher than the Dealer’s assumed value. h. The main rule is, ‘Never bet if you have more the 2 scores higher than the Dealer’s assumed Value’ unless you are playing for a Special such as having cards like: • Q, 7, K, Q- you should bet this because if your 5th card is a face card you win the 47 Special. • Similarly any three (3) face cards with a 8 or 9 must be played for the relevant special. • Four face cards is even better because now you have the chance of getting a 7, 8, 9 or another face card to win the relevant Special. Even if you end up with a ‘Spread’ ( 3, 4 of a kind or a Straight Flush) your cards will still add up to a low value. Dealer Specials: 1. The better special always wins. So’ if you hold a 1-3 Special and the Dealer holds a A-5, the Dealer wins. You only get paid the Bonus of $5000 and miss out on 20:1 payments. You lose your front and back bets but still get the Bonus. 2. Dealer Specials do not matter when players get 47, 48, 49 and 50 Specials.

const dealerShownValue = Logic.cardValue(dealerShown); const assumedDealerTotal = 20 + dealerShownValue; Object.values(this.gameState.players).forEach(p => { if (!p.isBot || p.folded || p.disqualified || p.decided) return; const playerValue = Logic.calculateHandValue(p.cards); const faceCount = p.cards.filter(Logic.isFaceCard).length; // 4 face cards: always play (chasing 47-50) if (faceCount === 4) { p.backBet = p.frontBet * 2; p.decided = true; p.result = "playing"; return; } // 3 face cards + 7/8/9: play for potential special if (faceCount === 3) { const nonFaceValues = p.cards.filter(c => !Logic.isFaceCard(c)).map(c => Logic.cardValue(c)); if (nonFaceValues.some(v => v >= 7 && v <= 9)) { p.backBet = p.frontBet * 2; p.decided = true; p.result = "playing"; return; } } const diff = playerValue - assumedDealerTotal; if (diff <= 0) { /* always bet */ } else if (diff <= 2) { /* probabilistic: 60% if diff=1, 30% if diff=2 */ } else { /* fold */ } }); } ``` - autoDecide() now calls this._botDecisions() before auto-folding undecided players - **G:\SipSam\PokerProject\.claude\worktrees\sad-haibt\rhum32-server\logic.js** - Added dealer special resolution system: ```javascript const SPECIAL_RANK = { 'Over 31': 0, '18-31 Normal': 1, '12-17 Special': 2, '8-11 Special': 3, '4-7 Special': 4, '1-5 Special': 5, '47 Special': 6, '48 Special': 7, '49 Special': 8, '50 Special': 9, '0 Special': 10, 'A-5 Special': 11 }; Scenario
Flow
Status
Full rounds complete (natural game over)
showGameOver() → fetch /api/game/exit
✅ Was already working

🆕 Fixed
What was broken:
Rhum32 client had no beforeunload handler at all — closing the tab silently abandoned the wallet.
The /api/game/exit-beacon endpoint referenced by the old SipSam client didn't exist on the server, so SipSam beacons were also hitting 404 (just silently failing).
What was added:
Server: new POST /api/game/exit-beacon?token=<jwt> endpoint in vurglife-platform/server/routes/game.js — validates the JWT from the query param (since sendBeacon can't set headers), credits remainingWallet to the user's bank.
Client: beforeunload listener in rhum32-client/game.js that fires navigator.sendBeacon with the live wallet amount — guarded by _rhum32IntentionalExit and _rhum32Settled flags to prevent double-crediting when the user clicks "Exit Game" or when the game ends naturally.
Cache bumped to game.js?v=22. Hard refresh (Ctrl+Shift+R) the rhum32 page.

The planned fix is to persist the entry walletSize in localStorage/sessionStorage when entering, and fall back to that value on the beacon if lastState is unreliable. 9. 1. Chip loss on refresh — fixed (rhum32-client/game.js, cache v23)
Root cause: the beforeunload beacon early-returned when lastState.players[mySessionId].wallet was 0/undefined. If the user refreshed before the first Colyseus state message arrived, no refund fired — they lost the walletSize they paid to sit down.
Fix:
Added _entryWallet global, populated from table.wallet (or table.walletSize, or the rhum32_wallet session key) in DOMContentLoaded.
The beforeunload handler now uses lastState.wallet when available, otherwise falls back to _entryWallet, so an early refresh still refunds the full entry amount.
After sending the beacon, the handler now sets _rhum32Settled = true and clears rhum32_user / rhum32_table / rhum32_wallet from sessionStorage so the reloaded tab doesn't double-enter the same table and doesn't re-fire the beacon on a fast double-refresh.
Bumped index.html cache: game.js?v=22 → v=23.
2. +2,000,000 chips granted (via vurglife-platform/scripts/grant-chips.js against data/vurglife.db, case-insensitive match):

how to test on mobile devices with the current setup?
Searched code
Quick honest answer: right now you can load the dashboard from a phone, but none of the games will work — the game clients all hardcode localhost for WebSockets, so a browser on another device tries to connect to itself and fails. Here are your options, from easiest to most productionlike:
Option 1 — Chrome DevTools device mode (zero setup)
Best for visual/layout testing on the same PC.
Open http://localhost:3000 in Chrome → F12 → click the phone icon (Ctrl+Shift+M).
Pick iPhone/Pixel presets, rotate, throttle network, simulate touch.
✅ Everything works (same origin, same localhost).
❌ Not a real device — doesn't catch iOS Safari quirks, real touch latency, or WebAudio unlock behavior.
Option 2 — Real phone over LAN (recommended for real testing)
Phone on the same WiFi as your PC connects to http://<PC-IP>:3000.
Step 1 — Find your PC's LAN IP
ipconfig | findstr IPv4
You'll see something like 192.168.1.42.
Step 2 — Open firewall ports
PowerShell as Admin:
New-NetFirewallRule -DisplayName "VurgLife Dev" -Direction Inbound -Protocol TCP -LocalPort 3000,3001,3002,3003,3004,2998,2999 -Action Allow
Step 3 — Fix hardcoded localhost in the game clients (blocker)
The four game clients all have lines like:
const SERVER_HTTP = "http://localhost:3000";
const SERVER_WS   = "ws://localhost:3003";
When loaded on a phone these resolve to the phone itself, so matchmake/WS fail. They need to derive host dynamically:
const SERVER_HTTP = `${location.protocol}//${location.hostname}:3000`;
const SERVER_WS   = `${location.protocol === 'https:' ? 'wss' : 'ws'}://${location.hostname}:3003`;
Files that need this fix:
rhum32-client/game.js (lines 9–10, WS port 3003)
poker-client/game.js (lines 9–10, WS port 3001)
poker-client/game(1).js (same)
…and the Blackjack (3002) and Hold'em (3004) clients if they do the same.
The platform server already binds to 0.0.0.0 via app.listen(PORT), so no server change is needed.
Step 4 — Connect
On the phone browser: http://192.168.1.42:3000. Log in normally.
Gotchas:
iOS Safari won't let navigator.sendBeacon fire to a hostname that differs from page origin — using location.hostname avoids that.
Web Audio must be unlocked by a user tap; your existing getAudioCtx() resume logic handles this.
Corporate/guest WiFi sometimes blocks peer-to-peer LAN traffic — use a personal router or phone hotspot.
Option 3 — Public tunnel (test away from LAN, share with friends)
Use a tunnel so you get a real https:// URL that works anywhere:
cloudflared (free, no account):
winget install --id Cloudflare.cloudflared
cloudflared tunnel --url http://localhost:3000
It prints something like https://abc-def-ghi.trycloudflare.com.
ngrok alternative:
winget install ngrok
ngrok http 3000
You still need the location.hostname fix from Step 3 — and additionally, the game WebSockets on 3001/3003/3004 won't be exposed by a single tunnel. You'd need:
Either run one tunnel per port (messy, multiple subdomains), or
Proxy the WebSockets through port 3000 using the existing platform server (http-proxy-middleware or upgrade handling), so everything goes through one tunnel. This is also how it would work in prod.
My recommendation
For quick iteration: Option 2 (LAN + location.hostname fix). It's 10 minutes of work and gives you a real phone on real touch with the exact dev server.
Want me to:
Apply the location.hostname fix to all four game clients right now, and
Set up a singleorigin WebSocket proxy on port 3000 so tunneling (Option 3) also works?
That pair of changes gives you all three testing modes without further wiring.

All four issues fixed and platform restarted. Summary:
1. SipSam invite "Server error" — fixed
Root cause: poker-client/game.js:1268 was POSTing to /api/game/invite, which doesn't exist. The real endpoint is /api/friends/invite and it requires a game field the client wasn't sending. Fix: pointed the fetch at /api/friends/invite and added game: 'sipsam' to the body.
Also hardened the server route (vurglife-platform/server/routes/friends.js:89): username lookup is now case-insensitive (COLLATE NOCASE), self-invites are rejected with a clean 400, and the friendship requirement is preserved per your follow-up — only friends can be invited to a game, as you stated.
2. Rhum32 table border — thicker, distinct color
Added two new CSS vars: --rail: #2d1810 (dark mahogany) and --rail-hi: #5a3520 (bevel highlight).
.felt-surface border changed from 2px solid var(--neon) (gold, blending into the glow) to 10px solid var(--rail) with a 1px bevel outline.
Gold underglow box-shadow is untouched — the halo, pulse animation, and .oval-table::before blurred radial all stay exactly as they were.
3. Rhum32 Friends Lobby — SipSam-style
New HTML roster block #friends-lobby-roster (index.html:177) with a PLAYERS IN LOBBY label and a seat list.
New CSS in style.css for .seat-row, .seat-host, .seat-open.
New _friendsLobbyOpen state flag in game.js.
pickMode('friends') now starts the Friends Lobby flow with the Start button labeled "CREATE LOBBY" instead of "START GAME".
New createFriendsLobby() function: connects to the server via joinRoom with mode: 'single' (no bot fill), does not send startGame, flips the button label to "START GAME", locks the rounds selector, and opens the roster.
startGame() is now a 2-click dance in Friends mode: first click creates the lobby, second click actually starts the game.
renderState() auto-renders the roster while status === 'waiting' and the lobby screen is active, for both the host and any invited joiners.
renderFriendsLobbyRoster(state) paints host + joined friends + "— Open Seat —" rows up to 6 seats.
autoJoinInviteRoom() (the path invited friends take) now also shows the roster so invitees see everyone waiting.
Invites already use currentRoomId, which is set by joinRoom(), so a friend accepting the invite lands in the exact same private room.
4. "Solo" removed from Rhum32
rhum32-client/index.html:86 "Play solo or open a private lobby…" → "Play single or…"
rhum32-client/index.html:106 "Play solo or invite your friends" → "Play single or invite your friends"
rhum32-client/game.js:342 status text "Pick rounds, then start solo" → "Pick rounds, then start single"
Confirmed zero remaining matches of Solo/SOLO/solo under rhum32-client/.

Let us do some work with SipSam while i thoroughly test Rhum32: 1. I have a major issue with sipsam. So i had 2 human players and 2 bots. When a human player left, a bot took over from the next round. However, the Bot did not play any hands. I ignored this for a while, but now i tested this when the human player was chosen randomly to be the Banker. When the human left the game, a bot replaced him for the next round that followed. Again the bot did not actively participate in the game so the rounds did not have any winners or losers. Do you understand what I am saying? The bots that replace humans must continue to play. Bots are allowed to go into a negative wallet, even as Bankers . However, human players who end up at $0 or less are evicted if they do not replenish their wallets on time. 2. I want to include Freeze bets just like the other games (Rhum32 and Blackjack). 3. Joining games do not work well. This is where Rhum32 is better. When a human player selects SipSam to play and choose a table, they automatically end up in any table that is available regardless of table limit. So if i am playing $500 table in a browser and then log in another browser and try to play $100 table with a different user, I still join the $500 table. This should not be so. Similar to Rhum32 and BlackJack, each game type, whether it be $100, $250, $500 or $1000, must be able to have numerous games running simultaneously. However, if a $500 game has bots and a human player wants to play a $500 game, then they should get in to play since the game should evict the bot. Human players have priority. Bots are fillers to keep the game running. If in this same scenario, the 2nd human player wants to play $250 game, then he should not enter the $500 game but be directed to a $250 game that has bots that he could replace or a new game will open up with him and bots as fillers. Do you understand these 3 fixes?

Updated todos
All three SipSam fixes are complete. Here's a summary:
Fix 1 — Matchmaking by Tier (was: all players land in same room)
Root cause: poker-server/index.js defaulted roomId to "sipsam_main" regardless of tableMinBet. A $250 player and a $500 player ended up in the same game.
Changes:
New file: poker-server/RoomManager.js — a SipSamRoomManager (mirrors the working Rhum32 RoomManager pattern). Rooms are keyed as sipsam_<tier>_<counter>_<timestamp>. The joinOrCreate(tableMinBet, maxRounds) method filters candidates by exact tier match and prefers rooms with waiting seats or evictable bots.
Rewritten: poker-server/index.js — now uses the RoomManager. The matchmake endpoint reads tableMinBet and maxRounds from the POST body and routes to the correct tier. Includes /tables/browse per-tier endpoint.
Updated: poker-client/game.js — joinRoom() now sends tableMinBet and maxRounds in the matchmake body. Removed all 'sipsam_main' fallback defaults.
Fix 2 — Bot Replacement (was: replacement bots don't play)
Root causes found & fixed:
5th-player bug: When the Banker left, the code created a new Bot_Banker entry AND kept the old player as a ghost with _promoteToRealBot=true, producing 5 players in a 4-seat game. Fix: The old banker's entry is now deleted outright since Bot_Banker fills the vacancy.
Lingering DQ flags: Ghost→bot promotion didn't clear debtDqd, disqualified, or disqualifyReason, so promoted bots could be permanently DQ'd. Fix: All flags are now explicitly reset during promotion.
Bot eviction on join: Humans now have priority — if a human joins a full table that has bots, a random bot is evicted to make room (matching the Rhum32 pattern).
Bot banker auto-accepts doubles: Added a 1.5s delayed auto-response for bot bankers (60% accept rate) on double-bet requests, since bot bankers have no WebSocket client.
Fix 3 — Freeze Bets (new feature)
Ported from Rhum32 pattern:
Server: Added frozen: false to player state, freezeBet message handler, freeze-guard in _onPlaceBet, frozen bet preservation between rounds in startRound().
Client: Added freeze/unfreeze toggle button in the bet overlay, _frozenBet state, _applyFreezeIfActive() at betting phase start, disabled +/- buttons when frozen.
Per your request: Freeze bets are cleared on game end — both server-side (endGame() sets all player.frozen = false) and client-side (_clearFreezeBet() fires on gameOver status). No localStorage persistence — freeze state is purely session-scoped and dies with the game.

I tied with the dealer in a Bust bet and did not get paid. Was it because of the bust?
Looking at your screenshot, both you and the dealer have a hand value of 40. The dealer busted (40 > 32), so the message says "Dealer busted with 40. You win front bet 1:1."
You did get paid — you won +$58,000. The dealer busting means you win your front bet regardless of your own hand value. That's the correct behavior per the rules: when the dealer crosses 32, all staying players win their front bet 1:1.
Your hand value of 40 is also over 32, but that doesn't matter when the dealer busts — the dealer busting takes priority and you collect.
So the payout is working correctly here. Is there something specific you expected to be different?
Yes, I am supposed to receive the Tie Bet payout as well.
